# <a name="office-365-education"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-105">Office 365 教育版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-105">Office 365 Education</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-106">为了最好地满足您的组织的需要，许多计划中都提供了 Microsoft Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-106">Microsoft Office 365 is available in a variety of plans to best meet the needs of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-107">如果你要查找教育计划Office 365差异，本文将介绍每个计划中包含的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-107">If you're looking for the differences between the Office 365 education plans, this article will show you which features are included in each of them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-108">Office 365 将熟悉的 Microsoft Office 桌面套件与 Microsoft 的下一代通信和协作服务（包括 &mdash; Microsoft Exchange Online、Microsoft Office SharePoint Online、Office 网页版和 Microsoft Skype for Business Online）的基于云的版本相结合，帮助用户从几乎任何位置通过 Internet 提高工作效率 &mdash; 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-108">Office 365 combines the familiar Microsoft Office desktop suite with cloud-based versions of Microsoft's next-generation communications and collaboration services&mdash;including Microsoft Exchange Online, Microsoft SharePoint Online, Office for the web, and Microsoft Skype for Business Online&mdash;to help users be productive from virtually anywhere through the internet.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="29410-109">本文列出了适用于教育Office 365计划 (A1、A3 和 A5) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-109">This article lists the features for Office 365 education plans (A1, A3, and A5).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-110">若要跨业务和企业计划比较功能，请参阅[比较 Office 365 for Business](https://www.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans)计划，或者有关功能的详细列表，请参阅 Microsoft 365 和 Office 365 服务说明下的相关[服务说明](../office-365-service-descriptions-technet-library.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-110">To compare features across business and enterprise plans, see [Compare Office 365 for Business plans](https://www.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans) or, for a more detailed list of features, see the relevant service description under [Microsoft 365 and Office 365 service descriptions](../office-365-service-descriptions-technet-library.md).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="29410-111">若要搜索支持文章和信息，请参阅Office[帮助 &amp; 培训](https://support.office.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-111">To search for support articles and information, see [Office Help &amp; Training](https://support.office.com/).</span></span>

## <a name="security-amp-compliance-center-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-637">安全 &amp; 与合规中心功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-637">Security &amp; Compliance Center features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-638">安全[ &amp; 与合规](/microsoft-365/compliance/go-to-the-securitycompliance-center)中心旨在帮助你管理组织中跨Office 365合规性功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-638">The [Security &amp; Compliance Center](/microsoft-365/compliance/go-to-the-securitycompliance-center) is designed to help you manage compliance features across Office 365 for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-639">Links to existing SharePoint and Exchange compliance features bring together compliance capabilities across Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-639">Links to existing SharePoint and Exchange compliance features bring together compliance capabilities across Office 365.</span></span> 
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-p120">Currently, many of the compliance features are still accessible through service-specific management interfaces, such as the Exchange admin center (EAC). <sup>5</sup> Microsoft Defender for Office 365 is available in Office 365 A5 and as a standalone service for Office 365 A1 and Office 365 A3.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="29410-724"><sup>6</sup>您还可以使用 Office 365[管理活动 API](/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference)从统一部署中检索审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-724"><sup>6</sup> You can also use the [Office 365 Management Activity API](/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference) to retrieve events from the unified audit log.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-928">下表提供了一些链接，这些链接指向Office教育计划中提供的 Web 功能Office 365功能与功能丰富的桌面Microsoft Office功能进行比较。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-928">The following table provides links to comparisons of Office for the web feature capabilities available in Office 365 education plans to feature-rich Microsoft Office desktop apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-929">使用比较可发现 Web Office中可用的功能，然后选择功能名称阅读有关该功能工作方式的简短说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-929">Use the comparisons to discover what features are available in Office for the web and then select the feature name to read a brief description about how that feature works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-930">你可能会发现，您的组织中的某些人员可能需要 Excel 桌面应用的高级图表功能，而其他人可能只需要使用 Office 网页版查看和轻松编辑 Word 文档和 PowerPoint 演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-930">You may discover that some people in your organization may need the advanced charting capability of the Excel desktop app while others may only need to view and lightly edit Word documents and PowerPoint presentations with Office for the web.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]

#### <a name="address-book-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1411">通讯簿限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1411">Address book limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1412">**地址列表** 限制 - 在 2013 年 10 月或 2013 Exchange Online中创建Exchange Server列表的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1412">**Address list limit** - The maximum number of address lists that can be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1413">此数目包括 Exchange Online 中的默认地址列表，如"所有联系人"和"所有组"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1413">This number includes the default address lists in Exchange Online, such as All Contacts and All Groups.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1414">**脱机通讯簿限制**- 在 (或) 2013 组织中Exchange Online或Exchange Server OAB 通讯簿的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1414">**Offline address book limit** - The maximum number of offline address books (OAB) that can be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1415">**通讯簿策略限制**- 在 (2013) 中创建的通讯簿策略Exchange Online Exchange Server数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1415">**Address book policies limit** - The maximum number of address book policies (ABP) that be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1416">**全局地址列表**- 在 (2013) 中创建的全局地址列表Exchange Online EXCHANGE SERVER数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1416">**Global address lists** - The maximum number of global address lists (GAL) that be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span>

#### <a name="mailbox-storage-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1437">邮箱存储限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1437">Mailbox storage limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-p144">可用邮箱存储量由邮箱类型和用户的订阅许可证决定。管理员可以减小每位用户或全局的最大邮箱大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p144">The amount of mailbox storage available is determined by the mailbox type and the user's subscription license. Administrators can reduce maximum mailbox sizes per user or globally.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1440">不允许使用日记、传输规则或自动转发规则将邮件复制到 Exchange Online 邮箱中来进行存档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1440">Using journaling, transport rules, or auto-forwarding rules to copy messages to an Exchange Online mailbox for the purposes of archiving is not permitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1441">用户的存档邮箱只供该用户使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1441">A user's archive mailbox is intended for just that user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1442">在用户存档邮箱用于存储其他用户的存档数据或其他不当使用的情况下，Microsoft 保留拒绝无限制存档的权利。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1442">Microsoft reserves the right to deny unlimited archiving in instances where a user's archive mailbox is used to store archive data for other users or in other cases of inappropriate use.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1475"><sup>1</sup> 每个用户最初都会获得 100 GB 的存档邮箱存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1475"><sup>1</sup> Each user initially receives 100 GB of storage in the archive mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1476">启用自动扩展存档后，只要达到 100 GB 存储容量，就会自动添加额外存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1476">When auto-expanding archiving is turned on, additional storage is automatically added when the 100 GB storage capacity is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1477">有关详细信息，请参阅 Overview of unlimited archiving in Office 365（Office 365 中的无限制存档概述）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1477">For more information, see Overview of unlimited archiving in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1478">有关可用性的详细信息，请参阅 Office 365 路线图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1478">See the Office 365 Roadmap for details about availability.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1479"> 
<sup>2</sup> 用户必须具有 Exchange Online 许可证才能访问共享邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1479"> 
<sup>2</sup> To access a shared mailbox, a user must have an Exchange Online license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1480">共享邮箱不需要单独的许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1480">Shared mailboxes don't require a separate license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1481">不过，如果要在共享邮箱上启用就地存档、就地保留或诉讼保留，必须具有 Exchange Online 计划 2 许可证或 Exchange Online 计划 1 和 Exchange Online Archiving 许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1481">However, if you want to enable In-Place Archive or put an In-Place Hold or a Litigation Hold on a shared mailbox, then an Exchange Online Plan 2 license or an Exchange Online Plan 1 with Exchange Online Archiving license is required.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1482">如果为共享邮箱启用就地存档和自动扩展存档，那么在达到存档邮箱的 100 GB 存储容量时就会自动添加额外存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1482">If you enable In-Place Archive and auto-expanding archiving for a shared mailbox, additional storage is automatically added when the 100 GB storage capacity for the archive mailbox is reached.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1483"> 
<sup>3</sup> 资源邮箱不需要许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1483"> 
<sup>3</sup> Resource mailboxes don't require a license.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1484"> 
<sup>4</sup> Site mailboxes are created and managed in SharePoint Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1484"> 
<sup>4</sup> Site mailboxes are created and managed in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1485">有关详细信息，请参阅准备在 Office 365 中使用网站邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1485">For more information, see Prepare for using site mailboxes in Office 365.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1486"> 
<sup>5</sup> 限制为 1000 个公用文件夹邮箱，所有公用文件夹邮箱的总大小上限为 50 TB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1486"> 
<sup>5</sup> You are limited to 1000 public folder mailboxes, and the maximum total size of all public folder mailboxes is 50 TB.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1487"> 
<sup>6</sup> In-Place 存档只能用于为单个用户或实体存档邮件 (例如已应用许可证) 共享邮箱邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1487"> 
<sup>6</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity (such as a shared mailbox) for which a license has been applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1488">禁止使用就地存档存储多个用户或实体的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1488">Using an In-Place Archive as a means of storing mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1489">例如，IT 管理员无法创建共享邮箱，也无法让用户复制（通过"抄送"或"密件抄送"字段，或通过传输规则）共享邮箱以便进行显式存档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1489">For example, an IT administrator can't create a shared mailbox and have users copy it (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a transport rule) for the explicit purpose of archiving.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1490">请注意，多个用户使用的共享邮箱实际上并不存储这些单个用户的电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1490">Note that a shared mailbox that multiple people use does not actually store email for those individual users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1491">多个用户拥有访问权限，且他们以共享邮箱发送电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1491">Multiple users have access, and they send email as the shared mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1492">因此，共享邮箱中仅存储以共享邮箱的名义往来发送的电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1492">Therefore, the only emails stored in the shared mailbox are those sent to or from it, as the shared mailbox.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1493"> 
<sup>7</sup> If you have created a retention policy in Exchange Online， messages will be automatically moved to a user's archive mailbox only if the user's primary mailbox is larger than 10 MB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1493"> 
<sup>7</sup> If you have created a retention policy in Exchange Online, messages will be automatically moved to a user's archive mailbox only if the user's primary mailbox is larger than 10 MB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1494">小于 10 MB 的邮箱不会自动运行保留策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1494">The retention policy will not run automatically for mailboxes that are smaller than 10 MB.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="capacity-alerts"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1495">容量报警</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1495">Capacity alerts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1496">Exchange Online 将在用户的邮箱接近或达到最大容量时提供三种通知类型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1496">Exchange Online provides three kinds of notifications when a user's mailbox is nearing, or at, capacity:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1497">**警告** - 用户收到一封电子邮件警告，指出邮箱接近最大大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1497">**Warning** - The user receives an email warning that the mailbox is approaching the maximum size limit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1498">此警告旨在建议用户删除不需要的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1498">This warning is intended to encourage users to delete unwanted mail.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1499">**禁止** 发送 - 达到邮箱大小限制时，用户会收到禁止发送的通知电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1499">**Prohibit Send** - The user receives a prohibit-send notification email when the mailbox size limit is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1500">在删除足够邮件以便邮箱低于大小限制之前，用户将无法发送新邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1500">The user cannot send new messages until enough email is deleted to bring the mailbox below the size limit.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1501">禁止 **发送/** 接收 - Exchange Online达到邮箱大小限制时拒绝任何传入邮件，并将未送达报告 (NDR) 发件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1501">**Prohibit Send/Receive** - Exchange Online rejects any incoming mail when the mailbox size limit is reached, and sends a non-delivery report (NDR) to the sender.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1502">发件人可选择稍后尝试重新发送该邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1502">The sender has the option to try resending the mail later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1503">若要再次接收邮件，用户必须删除邮件，直到邮箱的使用容量低于大小限制为止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1503">To receive messages again, the user must delete email until the mailbox is below the size limit.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="29410-1512">禁止发送</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1512">Prohibit Send</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29410-1513">49.5 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1513">49.5 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29410-1514">99 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1514">99 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29410-1515">99 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1515">99 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29410-1516">禁止发送/接收</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1516">Prohibit Send/Receive</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29410-1517">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1517">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29410-1518">100 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1518">100 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29410-1519">100 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1519">100 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
   
#### <a name="mailbox-folder-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1520">邮箱文件夹限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1520">Mailbox folder limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-p154">这些限制旨在将邮箱限制为在 Exchange Online 中受支持的已知尺寸。这些限制旨在防止文件夹中存在不限数量的邮箱项目，邮箱中存在不限数量的文件夹或 Exchange Online 组织中存在不限数量的公用文件夹。出于实用目的，邮箱文件夹限制实际上不受限制，足以支持大多数迁移到 Exchange Online 的 Exchange Online 邮箱和内部部署邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p154">These limits are intended to limit mailboxes to known dimensions that can be supported in Exchange Online. The goal of these limits is to prevent an infinite number of mailbox items per folder, an infinite number of folders per mailbox, or an infinite number of public folders per Exchange Online organization. For practical purposes, mailbox folder limits are in effect unlimited and sufficient to support most Exchange Online mailboxes and on-premises mailboxes that are migrated to Exchange Online.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1524">**每个邮箱文件夹的最大邮件数** - 指定邮箱文件夹的最大邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1524">**Maximum number of messages per mailbox folder** - Specifies the maximum number of messages for a mailbox folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1525">达到该限制时，无法将新邮件传递或保存到某个文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1525">New messages can't be delivered or saved in a folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1526">**每个邮箱文件夹** 的邮件数量的警告 - 指定邮箱文件夹在向邮箱所有者发送Exchange Online之前可以保留的邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1526">**Warning for number of messages per mailbox folder** - Specifies the number of messages that a mailbox folder can hold before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1527">达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1527">When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1528">**"可恢复** 邮件"文件夹中每个文件夹的邮件的最大数量 - 指定"可恢复邮件"文件夹的每个文件夹中可包含的最大邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1528">**Maximum number of messages per folder in the Recoverable Items folder** - Specifies the maximum number of messages that can be contained in each folder in the Recoverable Items folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1529">文件夹超出此限制时，将无法存储新邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1529">When a folder exceeds this limit, it can't store new messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1530">例如，如果"可恢复邮件"文件夹中的"删除"文件夹超出邮件计数限制，而邮箱所有者试图从邮箱中永久删除邮件，删除将会失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1530">For example, if the Deletions folder in the Recoverable Items folder has exceeded the message count limit and the mailbox owner attempts to permanently delete items from their mailbox, the deletion will fail.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1531">**"** 可恢复邮件"文件夹中每个文件夹的邮件数量的警告 - 指定"可恢复的项目"文件夹中每个文件夹在将事件记录到应用程序事件日志Exchange Online可以保留的邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1531">**Warning for number of messages per folder in the Recoverable Items folder** - Specifies the number of messages that each folder in the Recoverable Items folder can hold before Exchange Online logs an event to the application event log.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1532">**每个邮箱文件夹的子文件夹的最大数量** - 指定可以在邮箱文件夹中创建的子文件夹的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1532">**Maximum number of subfolders per mailbox folder** - Specifies the maximum number of subfolders that can be created in a mailbox folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1533">达到此限制时，邮箱所有者将无法创建新子文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1533">The mailbox owner won't be able to create a new subfolder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1534">**每个邮箱文件夹** 的子文件夹数量的警告 - 指定在 Exchange Online 向邮箱所有者发送警告消息之前可以在邮箱文件夹中创建的子文件夹的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1534">**Warning for number of subfolders per mailbox folder** - Specifies the number of subfolders that can be created in a mailbox folder before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1535">达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1535">When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1536">**最大文件夹层次结构深度** - 指定邮箱的文件夹层次结构中级别的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1536">**Maximum folder hierarchy depth** - Specifies the maximum number of levels in the folder hierarchy of a mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1537">达到此限制时，邮箱所有者将无法在邮箱文件夹的文件夹层次结构中创建另一个级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1537">The mailbox owner won't be able to create another level in the folder hierarchy of the mailbox folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1538">**文件夹层次结构深度** 警告 - 指定在 Exchange Online 向邮箱所有者发送警告消息之前，可以在邮箱文件夹的文件夹层次结构中创建的级别数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1538">**Warning for folder hierarchy depth** - Specifies the number of levels in the folder hierarchy of a mailbox folder that can be created before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1539">达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1539">When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1540">**公用文件夹的最大数量** - 指定完整公用文件夹层次结构中公用文件夹的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1540">**Maximum number of public folders** - Specifies the maximum number of public folders in the complete public folder hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1541">达到此限制后，必须删除现有公用文件夹，才可以创建新的公用文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1541">When this limit is reached, existing public folders must be deleted before new public folders can be created.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1542">**每个公用文件夹的** 子文件夹的最大数量 - 指定可以在公用文件夹中创建的子文件夹的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1542">**Maximum number of subfolders per public folder** - Specifies the maximum number of subfolders that can be created in a public folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1543">当达到此限制时，无法在公用文件夹中创建新的子文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1543">New subfolders can't be created in a public folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1544">**每个公用** 文件夹的子文件夹数量的警告 - 指定在 Exchange Online 向文件夹所有者发送警告消息之前可在公用文件夹中创建的子文件夹的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1544">**Warning for number of subfolders per public folder** - Specifies the number of subfolders that can be created in a public folder before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the folder owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1545">如果不存在所有者，则警告消息会发送到具有所有者权限的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1545">If no owner exists, warning messages are sent to users with Owner permissions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1546">达到此配额时，将每天发送一次警告消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1546">When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1611"><sup>1</sup> 您可以在用户之间发送和接收最多 150 MB 的邮件 (其中邮件永远不会离开 Microsoft 数据中心) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1611"><sup>1</sup> You can send and receive up to 150 MB messages between users (where the message never leaves the Microsoft datacenters).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1612">在 Microsoft 数据中心之外路由的邮件需要额外的 33% 翻译编码增加，在这种情况下，最大邮件大小为 112 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1612">Messages that are routed outside of the Microsoft datacenters are subject to an additional 33% translation encoding increase, in which case the maximum message size is 112 MB.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="message-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1613">邮件限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1613">Message limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1614">**邮件大小** 限制 - 邮件大小限制是防止大型邮件阻止传递其他邮件并影响所有用户的服务性能所必需的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1614">**Message size limit** - Message size limits are necessary to prevent large messages from blocking delivery of other messages and affecting service performance for all users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1615">这些限制包括一些附件，并且适用于组织范围的所有邮件（入站、出站和内部）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1615">These limits include attachments, and apply organization-wide to all messages (inbound, outbound, and internal).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1616">将不送达超过该限制的邮件，同时发件人将收到未送达报告 (NDR)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1616">Messages larger than this limit will not be delivered, and the sender will receive a non-delivery report (NDR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1617">尽管可以向上、向下或按每个用户配置邮件大小限制，但管理员仍可以创建传输规则以限制任何单个附件的最大大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1617">While message size limits can be configured up, down, or on a per-user basis, administrators can also create transport rules to limit the maximum size of any individual attachment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1618">若要了解其他信息，请参阅 microsoft [支持较大的电子邮件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2144144)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1618">To learn more, see [Microsoft supports larger email messages](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2144144).</span></span>
    
   > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="29410-1619">某些电子邮件客户端的邮件大小限制可能会更低，或者可能将单个文件附件的大小限制为小于 Exchange Online 邮件大小限制的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1619">Some email clients may have lower message size limits or may limit the size of an individual file attachment to a value that is less than the Exchange Online message size limit.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1620">**主题长度** 限制 - 电子邮件的主题行中允许的最大文本字符数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1620">**Subject length limit** - The maximum number of text characters allowed in the subject line of an email message.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1621">**文件附件** 限制 - 电子邮件中允许的最大文件附件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1621">**File attachments limit** - The maximum number of file attachments allowed in an email message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1622">即使所有文件附件的总大小并不违反邮件大小限制，邮件中允许的附件数量也仍具有限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1622">Even if the total size of all the file attachments doesn't violate the message size limit, there is still a limit on how many attachments are allowed in the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1623">限制由多部分邮件限制进行控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1623">This limit is controlled by the multipart message limit.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1624">**文件附件大小限制** - 单个附件的最大文件大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1624">**File attachment size limit** - The maximum file size of a single attachment.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE] 
    > <span data-ttu-id="29410-1625">此为单个附件的最大文件大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1625">This is the maximum file size of a single attachment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1626">单个客户端程序（包括 Outlook 网页）可能会将附件大小限制在此最大值以下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1626">Individual client programs, including Outlook on the web, may limit the size of attachments below this maximum.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1627">Exchange ActiveSync 不基于个别附件实施附件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1627">Exchange ActiveSync does not implement attachment size limits on an individual attachment basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1628">Exchange ActiveSync 邮件的所有附件总大小必须低于邮件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1628">The total size of all attachments to an Exchange ActiveSync message must be less than the message size limit.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1629">**多部分邮件限制** - MIME 多部分邮件中允许的邮件正文部分的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1629">**Multipart message limit** - The maximum number of message body parts that are allowed in a MIME multipart message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1630">此限制还会控制邮件中允许的文件附件的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1630">This limit also controls the maximum number of file attachments that are allowed in a message.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1631">**嵌入邮件深度** 限制 - 电子邮件中允许的最大转发电子邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1631">**Embedded message depth limit** - The maximum number of forwarded email messages that are allowed in an email message.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1688"><sup>1</sup> Microsoft 管理员可以指定 1 MB 到 150 MB 之间的自定义限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1688"><sup>1</sup> Microsoft administrators can specify a custom limit between 1 MB and 150 MB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1689">不过，你可以发送或接收的邮件大小还取决于你的电子邮件客户端或解决方案的支持范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1689">However, the size of message you can send or receive also depends on what your email client or solution supports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1690">有关为组织自定义最大允许邮件大小的信息，请参阅 [Microsoft支持更大电子邮件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2144144)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1690">For more information about customizing the maximum allowed message size for your organization, see [Microsoft supports larger email messages](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2144144).</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1691"> 
<sup>2</sup> 您可以在用户之间发送和接收最多 150 MB 的邮件 (其中邮件永远不会离开 Microsoft 数据中心) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1691"> 
<sup>2</sup> You can send and receive up to 150 MB messages between users (where the message never leaves the Microsoft datacenters).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1692">在 Microsoft 数据中心之外路由的邮件需要额外的 33% 翻译编码增加，在这种情况下，最大邮件大小为 112 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1692">Messages that are routed outside of the Microsoft datacenters are subject to an additional 33% translation encoding increase, in which case the maximum message size is 112 MB.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1693"> 
<sup>3</sup> OWA 帐户，因为邮件可能受 33% 编码增加影响，并将可发送的邮件大小限制到小于配置设置的 25%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1693"> 
<sup>3</sup> OWA accounts for the possibility that your message may be subject to the 33% encoding increase and restricts the size of message you can send to 25% less than the configured setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1694">例如，如果将设置自定义为 100 MB 最大邮件大小，则你可以发送不超过 75 MB 的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1694">For example, if you customize your settings for a 100 MB maximum message size, you can send messages no larger than 75 MB.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1695"> 
<sup>4</sup>要移动到邮件中Exchange Online的大小由Exchange Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1695"> 
<sup>4</sup> The size of messages to be moved into Exchange Online are computed by Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1696">Exchange Server 2013 之前的 Exchange 版本可能会报告较小的邮件大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1696">Versions of Exchange prior to Exchange Server 2013 may report a smaller item size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1697">此限制适用于使用任何受支持 Exchange 邮箱复制服务的基于移动的迁移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1697">This limit applies to move based migrations using any supported Exchange Mailbox Replication Service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1698">其他迁移方法（直接转换、暂存、IMAP、PST）和其他第三方工具具有常规邮件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1698">Other migration methods (Cutover, Staged, IMAP, PST) and other third-party tools are limited by the general message size limit.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="29410-1699">

#### <a name="receiving-and-sending-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1700">接收和发送限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1700">Receiving and sending limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-p174">接收和发送限制可用于防止出现垃圾邮件和大量邮件蠕虫或病毒。这些限制可以帮助保护系统的运行状况和我们用户的安全。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p174">Receiving and sending limits are applied to combat spam and mass-mailing worms or viruses. These limits help to protect the health of our systems and keep our users safe.</span></span>
  
#### <a name="receiving-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1703">接收限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1703">Receiving limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-p175">接收限制应用于用户、组或公用文件夹每小时可以接收的邮件数。这适用于从 Internet 和本地服务器收到的邮件。超出接收限制时，只要有电子邮件发送到此邮箱，都会收到未送达报告，指出邮箱已超出最大发送阈值。一个小时后，限制会进行刷新，邮箱将能够再次接收邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p175">Receiving limits apply to the number of messages that a user, group, or public folder can receive per hour. This applies for both messages received from the Internet and from on-premises servers. When the receiving limit has been exceeded, any emails sent to that mailbox will receive a non-delivery report stating that the mailbox has exceeded the maximum delivery threshold. After one hour, the limit will refresh and the mailbox will once again be able to receive messages.</span></span><br><br>

#### <a name="sending-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1716">发送限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1716">Sending limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1717">发送限制应用于收件人数、邮件数和用户可以从其 Exchange Online 帐户发送的每封邮件的收件人数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1717">Sending limits apply to the number of recipients, number of messages, and number of recipients per message that a user can send from their Exchange Online account.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-p176">对于存储在组织的通讯簿中的通讯组，这类组计数为一个收件人。对于存储在邮箱的“联系人”文件夹中的通讯组，单独计数组的各个成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p176">For distribution groups stored in an organization's address book, the group is counted as one recipient. For distribution groups stored in the Contacts folder of a mailbox, the members of the group are counted individually.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1720">**收件人速率** 限制 - 为了阻止发送未经请求的批量邮件，Exchange Online收件人限制来阻止用户和应用程序发送大量电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1720">**Recipient rate limit** - To discourage the delivery of unsolicited bulk messages, Exchange Online has recipient limits that prevent users and applications from sending large volumes of email.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1721">这些限制适用于每个用户的所有出站和内部邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1721">These limits are applied per-user to all outbound and internal messages.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="29410-1722">需要发送合法批量电子邮件的 Exchange Online 客户（例如，客户新闻通讯）应使用专门提供这些服务的第三方提供商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1722">Exchange Online customers who need to send legitimate bulk commercial email (for example, customer newsletters) should use third-party providers that specialize in these services.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1723">**收件人** 限制 - 这是单个电子邮件的"收件人："、"抄送："和"密件抄送："字段中允许的最大收件人数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1723">**Recipient limit** - This is the maximum number of recipients allowed in the To:, Cc:, and Bcc: fields for a single email message.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="29410-p178">出于收件人速率限制和收件人限制的目的，组织共享通讯簿中存储的通讯组作为一个收件人计数。在个人通讯列表中，每个收件人单独计数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p178">For the purposes of the recipient rate limit and the recipient limit, a distribution group that is stored in the organization's shared address book counts as one recipient. In a personal distribution list, each recipient is counted separately.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1726">**邮件速率** 限制 - 邮件速率限制确定用户可在指定时段内从Exchange Online帐户发送的邮件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1726">**Message rate limit** - Message rate limits determine how many messages a user can send from their Exchange Online account within a specified period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1727">此限制有助于防止单个发件人过多消耗系统资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1727">This limit helps prevent overconsumption of system resources by a single sender.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1728">如果用户提交邮件的速度超过了通过 SMTP 客户端提交邮件的限制，邮件将被拒绝，并且客户端将需要重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1728">If a user submits messages at a rate that exceeds the limit via SMTP client submission, the messages will be rejected and the client will need to retry.</span></span>

#### <a name="retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1751">保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1751">Retention limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1752">这些限制控制可以访问收件箱中特定文件夹中的项目的时间长度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1752">These limits control the length of time that items in specific folders in the Inbox can be accessed.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1753">**"已删除邮件"文件夹保留** 期 - 邮件在被自动删除之前可在"已删除邮件"文件夹中保留的最大天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1753">**Deleted Items folder retention period** - The maximum number of days that items can remain in the Deleted Items folder before they're automatically removed.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1754">**从"已删除** 邮件"文件夹中删除的项目的保留期 - 从"已删除邮件"文件夹中删除的项目在永久删除之前保留的最大天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1754">**Retention period for items removed from the Deleted Items folder** - The maximum numbers of days that items removed from the Deleted Items folder are retained before they're permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1755">**垃圾邮件文件夹保留期** - 邮件在被自动删除之前可在"垃圾邮件"文件夹中保留的最大天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1755">**Junk Email folder retention period** - The maximum number of days that items can remain in the Junk Email folder before they're automatically removed.</span></span>

#### <a name="distribution-group-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1774">通讯组限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1774">Distribution group limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1775">这些限制适用于组织的共享地址簿中的通讯组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1775">These limits apply to distribution groups in your organization's shared address book.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1776">**通讯组的最大成员数** - 通讯组扩展后确定收件人总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1776">**Maximum number of distribution group members** - The total recipient count is determined after distribution group expansion.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1777">**限制向大型通讯组发送邮件** - 包含此限制所指定数目的成员的通讯组必须配置传递管理或邮件审批选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1777">**Limit sending messages to large distribution groups** - Distribution groups that contain the number of members specified by this limit must have delivery management or message approval options configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1778">传递管理选项将指定一个允许向通讯组发送邮件的发件人的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1778">Delivery management specifies a list of senders who are allowed to send messages to the distribution group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1779">邮件审批选项将指定一个或多个必须审批发送到通讯组的所有邮件的审阅人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1779">Message approval specifies one or more moderators who must approve all messages sent to the distribution group.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1780">**大型通讯组的最大** 邮件大小 - 如果将一封邮件发送给 5，000 个或 5，000 多个收件人，则邮件大小不能超过此限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1780">**Maximum message size for large distribution groups** - If a message is sent to 5,000 or more recipients, the message size can't exceed this limit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1781">如果此邮件的大小超出此限制，则不会传递此邮件，并且发件人会收到一份未送达报告 (NDR)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1781">If the message size exceeds the limit, the message isn't delivered, and the sender receives a non-delivery report (NDR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1782">在通讯组扩展后确定总收件人计数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1782">The total recipient count is determined after distribution group expansion.</span></span> 
    
| <span data-ttu-id="29410-1783">功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1783">Feature</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="29410-1784">Office 365 A1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1784">Office 365 A1</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="29410-1785">Office 365 A3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1785">Office 365 A3</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="29410-1786">Office 365 A5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1786">Office 365 A5</span></span> |

#### <a name="journal-transport-and-inbox-rule-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1810">日记、传输和收件箱规则限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1810">Journal, transport, and inbox rule limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-p184">以下列表包含适用于日记规则、传输规则的限制（也称为组织范围规则）以及适用于收件箱规则的限制。收件箱规则由单个用户设置，并适用于该用户邮箱发送和接收的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p184">The following list includes limits that apply to journal rules, transport rules (also known as organization-wide rules), and limits that apply to Inbox rules. Inbox rules are set up by individual users and applied to messages sent and received by the individual user's mailbox.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1813">**日记规则的最大数目** - 组织中可存在的最大日记规则数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1813">**Maximum number of journal rules** - The maximum number of journal rules that can exist in the organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1814">**最大传输规则数** - 组织中可存在的最大规则数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1814">**Maximum number of transport rules** - The maximum number of rules that can exist in the organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1815">**单个传输规则的最大大小** - 单个传输规则中可以使用的最大字符数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1815">**Maximum size of an individual transport rule** - The maximum number of characters that can be used in a single transport rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1816">这些字符将在条件、例外和操作中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1816">The characters are used in the conditions, exceptions, and actions.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1817">**所有传输规则** 中使用的所有正则表达式的字符限制 - 组织的所有传输规则条件和例外中所有正则表达式使用的字符总数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1817">**Character limit for all regular expressions used in all transport rules** - The total number of characters used by all the regular expressions in all the transport rule conditions and exceptions in the organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1818">可具有少量使用长而复杂的正则表达式的规则，也可具有多个使用简单正则表达式的规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1818">You can have a few rules that use long and complex regular expressions, or you can have many rules that use simple regular expressions.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1819">**附件内容的** 扫描限制 - 传输规则条件允许检查邮件附件的内容，但仅检查从附件中提取的文本中的前 1 MB 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1819">**Scanning limits for attachment content** - The transport rule conditions let you examine the content of message attachments, but only the first 1 MB of the text extracted from an attachment is inspected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1820">1 MB 的限制指的是从附件中提取的文本，而不是附件的文件大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1820">This 1 MB limit refers to the text extracted from the attachment, not to the file size of the attachment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1821">例如，一个 2 MB 的文件可能包含小于 1 MB 的文本，因此将检查整个文本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1821">For example, a 2 MB file may contain less than 1 MB of text, so all of the text would be inspected</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1822">**所有传输规则** 向邮件添加的最大收件人数 - 当邮件由不同的传输规则处理时，只能向该邮件添加有限数量的收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1822">**Maximum number of recipients added to a message by all transport rules** - When a message is acted on by different transport rules, only a finite number of recipients can be added to the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1823">在达到此限制后，不会再向该邮件添加任何其余的收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1823">After the limit is reached, any remaining recipients aren't added to the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1824">此外，传输规则不能向邮件添加通讯组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1824">Also, distribution groups can't be added to a message by a transport rule.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1825">**转发者** 限制 - 可以使用重定向操作为收件箱或传输规则配置的最大收件人数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1825">**Forwardee limit** - The maximum number of recipients that can be configured for an inbox or transport rule with a redirecting action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1826">如果某个规则配置为将邮件重定向到比此数目多的收件人，则不应用该规则，任何满足该规则条件的邮件将不重定向到该规则中列出的任何收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1826">If a rule is configured to redirect a message to more than this number of recipients, the rule won't be applied and any message that satisfies the rule condition won't be redirected to any of the recipients listed in the rule.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1827">**邮件重定向次数** - 根据收件箱规则自动重定向、转发或答复邮件次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1827">**Number of times a message is redirected** - The number of times a message will be redirected, forwarded, or replied to automatically based on Inbox rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1828">例如，用户 A 有一个根据发件人将邮件重定向到用户 B 的收件箱规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1828">For example, User A has an Inbox rule that redirects messages to User B, based on the sender.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1829">用户 B 有一个根据主题行中的关键字将邮件转发到用户 C 的收件箱规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1829">User B has an Inbox rule that forwards messages to User C based on keywords in the subject line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1830">如果某邮件同时满足这两个条件，则由于仅允许一次重定向，该邮件仅发送到用户 B，不会转发到用户 C。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1830">If a message satisfies both of these conditions, the message is only sent to User B; it's not forwarded to User C because only one redirection is allowed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1831">在这种情况下，邮件将被丢弃，而不会向用户 B 发送未送达报告 (NDR) 以指明邮件未发送给用户 C。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1831">In this case, the message is dropped without sending a non-delivery report (NDR) to User B indicating that the message wasn't delivered to User C.</span></span>

#### <a name="moderation-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1868">审阅限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1868">Moderation limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1869">这些限制将控制用于适用于通讯组和传输规则的邮件审批的审阅设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1869">These limits control the moderation settings that are used for message approval applied to distribution groups and transport rules.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1870">**仲裁邮箱** 的最大大小 - 如果仲裁邮箱超过此限制，需要仲裁的邮件将返回到未送达报告 (NDR) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1870">**Maximum size of the arbitration mailbox** - If the arbitration mailbox exceeds this limit, messages that require moderation are returned to the sender in a non-delivery report (NDR).</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1871">**审阅人的最大** 数目 - 可分配给单个仲裁通讯组或可以使用单个传输规则添加到邮件的审阅人的最大数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1871">**Maximum number of moderators** - The maximum number of moderators that you can assign to a single moderated distribution group or that can be added to a message using a single transport rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1872">请注意，您不能将通讯组指定为审阅人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1872">Note that you can't specify a distribution group as a moderator.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1873">**等待审核的邮件的** 过期时间 - 默认情况下，等待审核的邮件在两天后过期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1873">**Expiration for messages waiting for moderation** - By default, a message waiting for moderation expires after two days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1874">但每 7 天将处理一次已过期的中继邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1874">However, the processing of expired moderated messages runs every seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1875">这意味着，中继邮件会在 2 到 9 天内随时过期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1875">This means that a moderated message can expire at any time between two and nine days.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1876">**过期的审核通知** 邮件的最大速率 - 此限制设置 1 小时内过期的已审核邮件的通知邮件的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1876">**Maximum rate for expired moderation notification messages** - This limit sets the maximum number of notification messages for expired moderated messages in a one-hour period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1877">对数据中心内的每个邮箱数据库施加了此限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1877">This limit is placed on each mailbox database in the datacenter.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="29410-p194">在使用率较高的时段内，一些发件人可能无法收到已过期的中继邮件的通知邮件。但仍可使用送达报告来发现这些通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-p194">During periods of heavy usage, some senders may not receive notification messages for moderated messages that have expired. However, these notifications are still discoverable using delivery reports.</span></span>

#### <a name="exchange-activesync-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1900">Exchange ActiveSync 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1900">Exchange ActiveSync limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1901">以下限制适用于 Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync，一个在移动设备和 Exchange 之间同步邮箱数据的客户端协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1901">The following limits apply to Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync, a client protocol that synchronizes mailbox data between mobile devices and Exchange.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1902">**Exchange ActiveSync设备限制**- 每个邮箱Exchange ActiveSync设备的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1902">**Exchange ActiveSync device limit** - The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices per mailbox.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1903">**Exchange ActiveSync删除限制**- Exchange ActiveSync管理员可以在一个月内Exchange删除的最大设备数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1903">**Exchange ActiveSync device deletion limit** - The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices that an Exchange administrator can delete in a single month.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-1904">**Exchange ActiveSync文件附件** 限制 - 邮件文件附件的最大大小，邮件文件附件可通过 Exchange ActiveSync 设备发送或接收。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1904">**Exchange ActiveSync file attachment limit** - The maximum size of a message file attachment that can be sent or received by an Exchange ActiveSync device.</span></span>

## <a name="onedrive-for-business-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1921">OneDrive for Business 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1921">OneDrive for Business features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-1922">OneDrive for Business (SkyDrive Pro) 云中的个人联机存储空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1922">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage space in the cloud.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1923">使用它，可以轻松、安全地跨多个设备存储工作文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1923">Use it to store your work files across multiple devices with ease and security.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1924">根据需要与同事共享文件，并实时Office Web Office编辑文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1924">Share your files with colleagues as needed, and edit Office documents together in real time with Office for the web.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1925">使用"同步"应用将文件OneDrive for Business本地计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1925">Sync files to your local computer using the OneDrive for Business sync app.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="29410-1926">OneDrive for Business 包含在 SharePoint Online 中，也可以作为独立的计划购买。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1926">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1927">"OneDrive for Business独立"选项Office Web 应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1927">The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office for the web.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29410-1928">若要了解更多信息，请参阅[什么是OneDrive for Business？。](https://support.office.com/article/187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1928">To learn more, see [What is OneDrive for Business?](https://support.office.com/article/187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076).</span></span>
  
### <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-1929">系统要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-1929">System Requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29410-2505">Skype for Business Online 中的限制分为以下几类：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2505">The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>

#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-2512">对等限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2512">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

#### <a name="meeting-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-2528">会议限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2528">Meeting limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2529">**文件上载** 限制 - 可上载到会议的最大文件大小，Skype for Business讲义和PowerPoint演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2529">**File upload limit** - The maximum size of files that can be uploaded to a Skype for Business meeting, including handouts and PowerPoint presentations.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2530">**会议参与者Skype for Business** - 会议的最大参与者 (包括演示者) 可以加入单个会议Skype for Business会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2530">**Participants in a Skype for Business meeting** - The maximum number of participants (including the presenter) who can join a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2531">**会议中的演示Skype for Business** - 单个会议中的演示者Skype for Business数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2531">**Presenters in a Skype for Business meeting** - The maximum number of presenters in a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2532">**Skype for Business Web 应用会议参与者**- Skype for Business可加入会议的最大 Web 应用会议参与者数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2532">**Skype for Business web app meeting participants** - The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can join a meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2533">**Skype for Business Web 应用匿名参与者**- 可匿名加入Skype for Business Web 应用会议参与者的最大数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2533">**Skype for Business web app anonymous participants** - The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can anonymously join a meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2534">**来宾通过电话加入** - 可以呼入会议的最大来宾数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2534">**Guests joining by phone** - The maximum number of guests who can call in to a meeting.</span></span>

#### <a name="meeting-retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29410-2570">会议保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2570">Meeting retention limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2571">**会议内容保留** 期 - 最后一个人离开会议后，任何上载的会议内容在永久删除之前Skype for Business保留的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2571">**Meeting content retention period** - The amount of time after the last person leaves a meeting that any uploaded meeting content is retained in Skype for Business before it is permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="29410-2572">**会议过期** 期限 - 会议结束后用户可以访问会议的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2572">**Meeting expiration period** - The amount of time after a meeting has ended that users can access the meeting.</span></span> 
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29410-2573">每个人在数据库中随时最多可拥有 1000 场会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29410-2573">Each person can have a maximum of 1000 conferences in the database at any time.</span></span>
